おいて	Conjunction:|1. at; in; on (Usually written using kana alone)
たるみ	Noun:|1. slack; slackening; sagginess; flabbiness (skin, etc.) (Usually written using kana alone)|2. dullness; letdown; depression; ennui (Usually written using kana alone)
ずらっと	Adverb:|1. in a line; in a row (Onomatopoeic or mimetic word)
棟	とう	Noun:|1. large building; building with a long roof||Suffix, Counter:|2. counter for buildings, apartments, etc.
